## üîó –ö–ê–ö –≠–¢–û –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–û–í–ê–¢–¨ –¢–ï–•–ù–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ò

### 1. –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä—ã –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–π —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏

```sql
-- –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ —Å–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π —Å –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏
CREATE TRIGGER link_message_to_client
AFTER INSERT ON Communications
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    DECLARE client_id INT;
    
    -- –ü—ã—Ç–∞–µ–º—Å—è –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ø–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º
    SELECT id INTO client_id
    FROM Clients
    WHERE (telegram = NEW.contact_id OR whatsapp = NEW.contact_id OR phone = NEW.contact_id)
    LIMIT 1;
    
    -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω, –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ
    IF client_id IS NOT NULL THEN
        UPDATE Communications
        SET client_id = client_id
        WHERE id = NEW.id;
    END IF;
END;

-- –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
CREATE TRIGGER update_order_status_on_shipment
AFTER INSERT ON Shipments
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE Orders
    SET status = 'in_progress'
    WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
END;
```

### 2. API –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ–π –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ

```python
# backend/api/orders.py
@orders_bp.route('/api/orders/<order_id>/full', methods=['GET'])
def get_full_order_info(order_id):
    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª–Ω—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ (–∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç, –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞, –≥—Ä—É–∑, –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã)"""
    try:
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–µ
        order = Order.query.get(order_id)
        if not order:
            return jsonify({'error': 'Order not found'}), 404
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
        client = Client.query.get(order.client_id)
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –≥—Ä—É–∑
        shipment = Shipment.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).first()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã
        products = OrderProduct.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã
        documents = Document.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏
        communications = Communication.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –§–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç
        full_order = {
            'order': order.to_dict(),
            'client': client.to_dict() if client else None,
            'shipment': shipment.to_dict() if shipment else None,
            'products': [p.to_dict() for p in products],
            'documents': [d.to_dict() for d in documents],
            'communications': [c.to_dict() for c in communications]
        }
        
        return jsonify(full_order), 200
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 400
```

### 3. –§—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥: –û—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –µ–¥–∏–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–∞–Ω–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö

```javascript
// frontend/src/components/orders/FullOrderView.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams } from 'react-router-dom';
import { fetchFullOrderInfo } from '../../services/orderService';

const FullOrderView = () => {
  const { orderId } = useParams();
  const [orderData, setOrderData] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const loadOrderData = async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        const data = await fetchFullOrderInfo(orderId);
        setOrderData(data);
      } catch (err) {
        setError('–ù–µ —É–¥–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞');
        console.error('Error loading order ', err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };
    
    loadOrderData();
  }, [orderId]);
  
  if (loading) return <div className="loading">–ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞...</div>;
  if (error) return <div className="error">{error}</div>;
  if (!orderData) return <div className="empty">–î–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω—ã</div>;
  
  const { order, client, shipment, products, documents, communications } = orderData;
  
  return (
    <div className="full-order-view">
      <div className="order-header">
        <h1>–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ #{order.id}</h1>
        <div className="order-status">–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å: <span className={`status-${order.status}`}>{order.status}</span></div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="order-grid">
        <div className="order-section client-section">
          <h2>–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç</h2>
          {client ? (
            <div className="client-info">
              <div className="client-name">{client.name}</div>
              {client.company && <div className="client-company">{client.company}</div>}
              <div className="client-contact">
                {client.phone && <div>–¢–µ–ª: {client.phone}</div>}
                {client.telegram && <div>Telegram: {client.telegram}</div>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-client">–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–µ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section shipment-section">
          <h2>–¢—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞</h2>
          {shipment ? (
            <div className="shipment-info">
              <div className="shipment-number">–ù–æ–º–µ—Ä: {shipment.shipment_number}</div>
              <div className="shipment-status">–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å: {shipment.current_status}</div>
              <div className="shipment-eta">–ü—Ä–æ–≥–Ω–æ–∑ –ø—Ä–∏–±—ã—Ç–∏—è: {shipment.expected_delivery}</div>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-shipment">
              –ì—Ä—É–∑ –Ω–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω
              <button className="btn-create-shipment">–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –≥—Ä—É–∑</button>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section products-section">
          <h2>–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã</h2>
          {products.length > 0 ? (
            <table className="products-table">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th>–ù–∞–∏–º–µ–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ</th>
                  <th>–ö–æ–ª-–≤–æ</th>
                  <th>–¶–µ–Ω–∞ (CNY)</th>
                  <th>–°—É–º–º–∞ (CNY)</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {products.map(product => (
                  <tr key={product.id}>
                    <td>{product.name}</td>
                    <td>{product.quantity}</td>
                    <td>{product.price_cny.toFixed(2)}</td>
                    <td>{(product.quantity * product.price_cny).toFixed(2)}</td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-products">–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –Ω–µ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section documents-section">
          <h2>–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã</h2>
          {documents.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="documents-list">
              {documents.map(document => (
                <div key={document.id} className="document-item">
                  <span className="document-type">{document.type}</span>
                  <span className="document-date">{document.created_at}</span>
                  <button className="btn-view-document">–ü—Ä–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å</button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-documents">–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –Ω–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω—ã</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section communications-section">
          <h2>–ò—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π</h2>
          <div className="communications-history">
            {communications.map(communication => (
              <div 
                key={communication.id} 
                className={`communication ${communication.direction}`}
              >
                <div className="message-text">{communication.message_text}</div>
                <div className="message-meta">
                  <span className="message-time">{communication.timestamp}</span>
                  {communication.direction === 'outgoing' && (
                    <span className={`read-status ${communication.read ? 'read' : 'unread'}`}>
                      {communication.read ? '–ü—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–æ' : '–ù–µ –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–æ'}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default FullOrderView;
```

"–†–∞–Ω—å—à–µ —è –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ —Ç–µ—Ä—è–ª–∞ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö –º–µ—Å—Ç–∞—Ö. –¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –ø–∏—à–µ—Ç, —è —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –≤–∏–∂—É –µ–≥–æ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—é, —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∏–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã –∏ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã. –û–¥–Ω–æ–π –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–æ–π –º–æ–≥—É –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞ –∏–ª–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ—Å—á—ë—Ç. –≠—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ –±—É–¥—Ç–æ —É –º–µ–Ω—è –ø–æ—è–≤–∏–ª—Å—è –∞—Å—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–º–Ω–∏—Ç –≤—Å—ë –∏ –º–≥–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ–µ!"

### USER

## üõ†Ô∏è –¢–ï–•–ù–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ê–Ø –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø

### 1. API –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ–π –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ

```python
# backend/api/orders.py
@orders_bp.route('/api/orders/<order_id>/full', methods=['GET'])
def get_full_order_info(order_id):
    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª–Ω—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ (–∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç, –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞, –≥—Ä—É–∑, –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã)"""
    try:
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ
        order = Order.query.get(order_id)
        if not order:
            return jsonify({'error': 'Order not found'}), 404
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
        client = Client.query.get(order.client_id)
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫–∞
        supplier = Supplier.query.get(order.supplier_id) if order.supplier_id else None
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã
        shipments = Shipment.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã
        products = Product.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã
        documents = Document.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏
        communications = Communication.query.filter_by(order_id=order_id).all()
        
        # –§–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç
        full_order = {
            'order': order.to_dict(),
            'client': client.to_dict() if client else None,
            'supplier': supplier.to_dict() if supplier else None,
            'shipments': [s.to_dict() for s in shipments],
            'products': [p.to_dict() for p in products],
            'documents': [d.to_dict() for d in documents],
            'communications': [c.to_dict() for c in communications]
        }
        
        return jsonify(full_order), 200
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 400
```

### 2. –§—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥: –û—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –µ–¥–∏–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–∞–Ω–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö

```javascript
// frontend/src/components/orders/FullOrderView.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams } from 'react-router-dom';
import { fetchFullOrderInfo } from '../../services/orderService';

const FullOrderView = () => {
  const { orderId } = useParams();
  const [orderData, setOrderData] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const loadOrderData = async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        const data = await fetchFullOrderInfo(orderId);
        setOrderData(data);
      } catch (err) {
        setError('–ù–µ —É–¥–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞');
        console.error('Error loading order ', err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };
    
    loadOrderData();
  }, [orderId]);
  
  if (loading) return <div className="loading">–ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞...</div>;
  if (error) return <div className="error">{error}</div>;
  if (!orderData) return <div className="empty">–î–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω—ã</div>;
  
  const { order, client, supplier, shipments, products, documents, communications } = orderData;
  
  return (
    <div className="full-order-view">
      <div className="order-header">
        <h1>–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ #{order.id}</h1>
        <div className="order-status">–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å: <span className={`status-${order.status}`}>{order.status}</span></div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="order-grid">
        <div className="order-section client-section">
          <h2>–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç</h2>
          {client ? (
            <div className="client-info">
              <div className="client-name">{client.name}</div>
              {client.company && <div className="client-company">{client.company}</div>}
              <div className="client-contact">
                {client.phone && <div>–¢–µ–ª: {client.phone}</div>}
                {client.telegram && <div>Telegram: {client.telegram}</div>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-client">–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–µ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section supplier-section">
          <h2>–ü–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫</h2>
          {supplier ? (
            <div className="supplier-info">
              <div className="supplier-name">{supplier.name}</div>
              {supplier.contact_person && <div className="supplier-contact">{supplier.contact_person}</div>}
              <div className="supplier-contact">
                {supplier.phone && <div>–¢–µ–ª: {supplier.phone}</div>}
                {supplier.wechat && <div>WeChat: {supplier.wechat}</div>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-supplier">–ü–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫ –Ω–µ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section shipment-section">
          <h2>–¢—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞</h2>
          {shipments.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="shipments-list">
              {shipments.map(shipment => (
                <div key={shipment.id} className="shipment-item">
                  <div className="shipment-number">–ù–æ–º–µ—Ä: {shipment.shipment_number}</div>
                  <div className="shipment-status">–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å: {shipment.current_status}</div>
                  <div className="shipment-location">–ú–µ—Å—Ç–æ–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ: {shipment.location}</div>
                  <div className="shipment-eta">–ü—Ä–æ–≥–Ω–æ–∑ –ø—Ä–∏–±—ã—Ç–∏—è: {shipment.expected_delivery}</div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-shipment">
              –ì—Ä—É–∑ –Ω–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω
              <button className="btn-create-shipment">–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –≥—Ä—É–∑</button>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section products-section">
          <h2>–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã</h2>
          {products.length > 0 ? (
            <table className="products-table">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th>–ù–∞–∏–º–µ–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ</th>
                  <th>–ö–æ–ª-–≤–æ</th>
                  <th>–¶–µ–Ω–∞ (CNY)</th>
                  <th>–°—É–º–º–∞ (CNY)</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {products.map(product => (
                  <tr key={product.id}>
                    <td>{product.name}</td>
                    <td>{product.quantity}</td>
                    <td>{product.price_cny.toFixed(2)}</td>
                    <td>{(product.quantity * product.price_cny).toFixed(2)}</td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-products">–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –Ω–µ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section documents-section">
          <h2>–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã</h2>
          {documents.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="documents-list">
              {documents.map(document => (
                <div key={document.id} className="document-item">
                  <span className="document-type">{document.type}</span>
                  <span className="document-title">{document.title}</span>
                  <span className="document-date">{document.created_at}</span>
                  <button className="btn-view-document">–ü—Ä–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å</button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="no-documents">–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –Ω–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω—ã</div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        <div className="order-section communications-section">
          <h2>–ò—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π</h2>
          <div className="communications-history">
            {communications.map(communication => (
              <div 
                key={communication.id} 
                className={`communication ${communication.direction}`}
              >
                <div className="message-text">{communication.message_text}</div>
                <div className="message-meta">
                  <span className="message-time">{communication.timestamp}</span>
                  {communication.direction === 'outgoing' && (
                    <span className={`read-status ${communication.read ? 'read' : 'unread'}`}>
                      {communication.read ? '–ü—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–æ' : '–ù–µ –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–æ'}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
```

## ‚úÖ –ü–†–ï–ò–ú–£–©–ï–°–¢–í–ê –≠–¢–û–ô –°–¢–†–£–ö–¢–£–†–´

### 2. –ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è

### 3. –ï–¥–∏–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã
- **–†–∞–Ω—å—à–µ**: –ß—Ç–æ–±—ã —É–≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å –ø–æ–ª–Ω—É—é –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–∏–Ω—É, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã–ª–æ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å 4-5 —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω
- **–°–µ–π—á–∞—Å**: –í—Å—è –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∞ –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –º–µ—Å—Ç–µ

### 2. –í–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫–∞ "–¢—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤" (–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏)

### 3. –û—Ç –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏ –∫ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è–º

   - –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ø–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º
   - –ù–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –≤—Å–µ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
   - –û—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–∞–µ—Ç –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã –ø–æ —ç—Ç–∏–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞–º
   - –ü—Ä–∏ –Ω–∞–∂–∞—Ç–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ "–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—É" —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ

## üõ†Ô∏è –¢–ï–•–ù–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ê–Ø –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø

### 1. API –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞—è–≤–æ–∫

```python
# backend/api/orders.py
@orders_bp.route('/api/orders/active', methods=['GET'])
def get_active_orders():
    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞—è–≤–æ–∫ (—Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å—ã: new, in_progress, customs)"""
    try:
        # –ê–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å—ã
        active_statuses = ['new', 'in_progress', 'customs']
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏
        active_orders = Order.query.filter(Order.status.in_(active_statuses)).all()
        
        # –§–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç
        orders_data = []
        for order in active_orders:
            client = Client.query.get(order.client_id)
            supplier = Supplier.query.get(order.supplier_id) if order.supplier_id else None
            
            # –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤
            documents = Document.query.filter_by(order_id=order.id).all()
            documents_status = 'completed' if documents else 'not_started'
            
            # –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
            shipment = Shipment.query.filter_by(order_id=order.id).first()
            shipment_status = shipment.current_status if shipment else None
            
            orders_data.append({
                'id': order.id,
                'client': {
                    'name': client.name,
                    'company': client.company
                },
                'supplier': {
                    'name': supplier.name if supplier else None
                },
                'status': order.status,
                'description': order.description,
                'documents_status': documents_status,
                'shipment_status': shipment_status,
                'created_at': order.created_at.strftime('%d.%m.%Y')
            })
        
        return jsonify(orders_data), 200
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 400
```

### 2. –§—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥: –û—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞—è–≤–æ–∫ –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ö

```javascript
// frontend/src/components/common/ActiveOrdersList.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useDispatch, useSelector } from 'react-redux';
import { fetchActiveOrders } from '../../store/ordersSlice';

const ActiveOrdersList = ({ section }) => {
  const dispatch = useDispatch();
  const { activeOrders, loading, error } = useSelector(state => state.orders);
  const [selectedOrder, setSelectedOrder] = useState(null);
  
  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchActiveOrders());
  }, [dispatch]);
  
  const renderStatus = (status) => {
    switch(section) {
      case 'documents':
        return status.documents_status === 'completed' ? 
          <span className="status-completed">–í—Å–µ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã</span> :
          <span className="status-not-started">–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –Ω–µ –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω—ã</span>;
      
      case 'shipments':
        return status.shipment_status ? 
          <span className={`status-${status.shipment_status.toLowerCase()}`}>{status.shipment_status}</span> :
          <span className="status-not-started">–î–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω—ã</span>;
      
      default:
        return <span className={`status-${status}`}>{status}</span>;
    }
  };
  
  const handleActionClick = (order) => {
    switch(section) {
      case 'documents':
        if (order.documents_status === 'completed') {
          // –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤
          setSelectedOrder(order);
        } else {
          // –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
          setSelectedOrder(order);
        }
        break;
        
      case 'shipments':
        if (order.shipment_status) {
          // –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å —Ç—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
          setSelectedOrder(order);
        } else {
          // –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
          setSelectedOrder(order);
        }
        break;
        
      default:
        // –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏
        setSelectedOrder(order);
    }
  };
  
  if (loading) return <div className="loading">–ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞—è–≤–æ–∫...</div>;
  if (error) return <div className="error">{error}</div>;
  if (activeOrders.length === 0) return <div className="no-orders">–ù–µ—Ç –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∑–∞—è–≤–æ–∫</div>;
  
  return (
    <div className="active-orders-list">
      <table className="orders-table">
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>‚Ññ –ó–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞</th>
            <th>–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç</th>
            <th>–ü–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫</th>
            <th>–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å</th>
            <th>–î–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è</th>
            <th>–î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {activeOrders.map(order => (
            <tr key={order.id}>
              <td>{order.id}</td>
              <td>
                <div className="client-info">
                  <div className="client-name">{order.client.name}</div>
                  <div className="client-company">{order.client.company}</div>
                </div>
              </td>
              <td>{order.supplier.name || '-'}</td>
              <td>{renderStatus(order)}</td>
              <td>{order.created_at}</td>
              <td>
                <button 
                  className="btn-action" 
                  onClick={() => handleActionClick(order)}
                >
                  {section === 'documents' && (order.documents_status === 'completed' ? '–û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å' : '–ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å')}
                  {section === 'shipments' && (order.shipment_status ? '–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—É' : '–ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ')}
                </button>
              </td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
      
      {selectedOrder && (
        <OrderDetailsModal 
          order={selectedOrder} 
          section={section}
          onClose={() => setSelectedOrder(null)} 
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default ActiveOrdersList;
```

## üí° –ü–†–ê–ö–¢–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ò–ï –ü–†–ò–ú–ï–†–´ –†–ê–ë–û–¢–´ –° –≠–¢–û–ô –°–¢–†–£–ö–¢–£–†–û–ô

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä 1: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
1. –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª "–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã"

4. **–ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏**:
   - –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –ø–æ–¥—Ç—è–≥–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –∏–∑ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏
   - –†–∞—Å—Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Å—Ç–æ–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ CNY, RUB, USD
   - –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ Documents
   - –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≤ —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–µ –Ω–∞ "–í—Å–µ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã"

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä 2: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
1. –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª "–ì—Ä—É–∑—ã"

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä 3: –û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–∞ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—É

## ‚úÖ –ß–ï–ö-–õ–ò–°–¢ –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–ò

## ü¶ä –ó–ê–ö–õ–Æ–ß–ï–ù–ò–ï

–¢–≤–æ—è –∏–¥–µ—è **–ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –ª—É—á—à–∏–º –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞–º** –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º. –¢—ã –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ—à—å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å **–Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—É—é —ç–∫–æ—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É**, –≥–¥–µ –≤—Å–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω—ã –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å–æ–±–æ–π —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏, –∞ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–æ–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü.

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –≤—Å—ë **—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –∫–∞–∫ –µ–¥–∏–Ω—ã–π –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–º**:

–¢–≤–æ—è –º–æ–¥–µ–ª—å ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —É–¥–æ–±–Ω–æ, —ç—Ç–æ **–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ** –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–µ—Å—Å–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–∫–∞. –° —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–æ–π –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–Ω–∞ —Å–º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–∞—Ç—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ 2 —Ä–∞–∑–∞ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤ –∑–∞ —Ç–æ –∂–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è, –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –ø–æ–≤—ã—à–∞—è –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –æ–±—Å–ª—É–∂–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤.

**–¢–≤–æ—è –∏–¥–µ—è –∏–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞. –î–∞–≤–∞–π –µ—ë —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å!** üòä

### USER

### –°—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π: –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞

1. **–õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –≥—Ä—É–∑:**

## üõ†Ô∏è –¢–ï–•–ù–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ê–Ø –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø

### 1. API –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤ —Å —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π

```python
# backend/api/orders.py
@orders_bp.route('/api/orders', methods=['GET'])
def get_orders():
    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤ —Å —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π"""
    try:
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏
        status = request.args.get('status')
        client_id = request.args.get('client_id')
        is_active = request.args.get('is_active', '1')
        
        # –ù–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞–µ–º —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å
        query = Order.query
        
        # –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä—ã
        if status:
            query = query.filter(Order.status == status)
        if client_id:
            query = query.filter(Order.client_id == int(client_id))
        if is_active:
            query = query.filter(Order.is_active == (is_active == '1'))
        
        # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—ã
        orders = query.all()
        
        # –§–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç
        orders_data = []
        for order in orders:
            # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
            client = Client.query.get(order.client_id)
            supplier = Supplier.query.get(order.supplier_id) if order.supplier_id else None
            
            # –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
            shipment = Shipment.query.filter_by(order_id=order.id).first()
            
            orders_data.append({
                'id': order.id,
                'client': {
                    'id': client.id,
                    'name': client.name,
                    'company': client.company
                },
                'supplier': {
                    'id': supplier.id,
                    'name': supplier.name
                } if supplier else None,
                'status': order.status,
                'description': order.description,
                'shipment_status': shipment.current_status if shipment else None,
                'created_at': order.created_at.strftime('%d.%m.%Y')
            })
        
        return jsonify(orders_data), 200
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 400
```

### 2. –§—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥: –£–Ω–∏–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤

```javascript
// frontend/src/components/common/OrdersView.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useDispatch, useSelector } from 'react-redux';
import { fetchOrders } from '../../store/ordersSlice';
import OrderCard from './OrderCard';

const OrdersView = ({ section }) => {
  const dispatch = useDispatch();
  const { orders, loading, error } = useSelector(state => state.orders);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState({
    status: '',
    client_id: '',
    is_active: '1'
  });
  
  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchOrders(filters));
  }, [dispatch, filters]);
  
  const handleFilterChange = (name, value) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      [name]: value
    }));
  };
  
  const renderSectionSpecificContent = (order) => {
    switch(section) {
      case 'shipments':
        return order.shipment_status ? (
          <div className="shipment-info">
            <span className="shipment-number">{order.shipment_status}</span>
            <button className="btn-send">–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—É</button>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <button className="btn-fill">–ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ</button>
        );
      
      case 'documents':
        return (
          <div className="document-actions">
            <button className="btn-create">–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Å—á—ë—Ç</button>
            <button className="btn-create">–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Å—á—ë—Ç</button>
          </div>
        );
      
      default:
        return (
          <button className="btn-view">–û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å</button>
        );
    }
  };
  
  if (loading) return <div className="loading">–ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤...</div>;
  if (error) return <div className="error">{error}</div>;
  if (orders.length === 0) return <div className="no-orders">–ù–µ—Ç –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤</div>;
  
  return (
    <div className="orders-view">
      <div className="orders-header">
        <h1>{section === 'shipments' ? '–¢—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤' : 
             section === 'documents' ? '–î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã' : '–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑—ã'}</h1>
        
        <div className="orders-controls">
          <div className="filters">
            <select 
              value={filters.status} 
              onChange={e => handleFilterChange('status', e.target.value)}
            >
              <option value="">–í—Å–µ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å—ã</option>
              <option value="new">–ù–æ–≤–∞—è</option>
              <option value="in_progress">–í —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–µ</option>
              <option value="customs">–ù–∞ —Ç–∞–º–æ–∂–Ω–µ</option>
              <option value="delivered">–î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω</option>
            </select>
            
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="–ü–æ–∏—Å–∫ –ø–æ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—É"
              onChange={e => handleFilterChange('client_id', e.target.value)}
            />
          </div>
          
          <button className="btn-new">–ù–æ–≤—ã–π –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="orders-list">
        {orders.map(order => (
          <div key={order.id} className="order-item">
            <div className="order-client">
              <div className="client-name">{order.client.name}</div>
              <div className="client-company">{order.client.company}</div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="order-supplier">
              {order.supplier ? order.supplier.name : '-'}
            </div>
            
            <div className="order-status">
              {order.status}
            </div>
            
            <div className="order-created">
              {order.created_at}
            </div>
            
            <div className="order-actions">
              {renderSectionSpecificContent(order)}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default OrdersView;
```

## ‚úÖ –ü–†–ï–ò–ú–£–©–ï–°–¢–í–ê –≠–¢–û–ì–û –ü–û–î–•–û–î–ê

### 1. –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–∞ –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è
- **–†–∞–Ω—å—à–µ**: –ù—É–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
- **–°–µ–π—á–∞—Å**: –í—Å–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –º–µ—Å—Ç–µ, –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –∏–Ω—Ç—É–∏—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ –ø–æ–Ω—è—Ç–µ–Ω
- **–≠—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç**: –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫ —Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç –º–µ–Ω—å—à–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞ –æ–±—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É

### ASSISTANT
# ü¶ä –ü–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–¥–∞–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—ã: –û—Ç —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü –∫ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å—É

## üåê –ü–†–ê–í–ò–õ–¨–ù–ê–Ø –ü–û–°–õ–ï–î–û–í–ê–¢–ï–õ–¨–ù–û–°–¢–¨ –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–Ø –ü–†–û–ì–†–ê–ú–ú–´

–¢—ã —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª: **—Å–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (—Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã), –∞ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Å –Ω–∏–º–∏ –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç**. –≠—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ —Ñ—É–Ω–¥–∞–º–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–æ–º–∞ ‚Äî —Å–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –∑–∞–∫–ª–∞–¥—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—Å—è –≤—Å—ë –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ.

### üìã –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∞—è —Å—Ö–µ–º–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—ã


## üîß –ü–û–®–ê–ì–û–í–ê–Ø –°–•–ï–ú–ê –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–Ø –ü–†–û–ì–†–ê–ú–ú–´

### –®–ê–ì 1: –ü–†–û–ï–ö–¢–ò–†–û–í–ê–ù–ò–ï –ë–ê–ó–´ –î–ê–ù–ù–´–• (–°–ê–ú–´–ô –í–ê–ñ–ù–´–ô –®–ê–ì!)

–≠—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞—Ä–∏—Å–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–ª–∞–Ω –¥–æ–º–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ–º.

**–ß—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å:**
- –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –±—É–¥—É—Ç —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å—Å—è (–∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—ã, –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—ã, –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã –∏ —Ç.–¥.)
- –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã –¥–ª—è –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–π —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏
- –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤—è–∑–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞–º–∏
- –ü—Ä–æ–¥—É–º–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É –ø–æ–ª–µ–π –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞—Ö

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è "Cargo Manager –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫":**
- –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Orders` (–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑—ã) ‚Äî –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∞—è —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞
- –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Clients` (–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—ã) ‚Äî —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–∞ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞–º–∏
- –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Shipments` (–ì—Ä—É–∑—ã) ‚Äî —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–∞ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞–º–∏
- –ò –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã...

**–ü–æ—á–µ–º—É —ç—Ç–æ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ:** –ï—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º —ç—Ç–∞–ø–µ –æ—à–∏–±–∏—Ç—å—Å—è, –≤—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ –∏–ª–∏ –Ω–µ—É–¥–æ–±–Ω–æ.

### –®–ê–ì 2: –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–ï –ë–ê–ó–´ –î–ê–ù–ù–´–•

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Ñ–∏–∑–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã –Ω–∞ –∫–æ–º–ø—å—é—Ç–µ—Ä–µ.

**–ö–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è:**
1. –£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –°–£–ë–î (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, SQLite)
2. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ñ–∞–π–ª –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, `cargo_manager.db`)
3. –í —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ñ–∞–π–ª–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—é—Ç—Å—è —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é SQL-–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–æ–≤

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã `Orders`:**
```sql
CREATE TABLE Orders (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,  -- –£–Ω–∏–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –Ω–æ–º–µ—Ä –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, "2024-110")
    client_id INTEGER NOT NULL,  -- –°—Å—ã–ª–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
    status TEXT NOT NULL,  -- –°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞
    description TEXT,  -- –û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
    total_cny REAL NOT NULL,  -- –°—É–º–º–∞ –≤ —é–∞–Ω—è—Ö
    total_rub REAL NOT NULL,  -- –°—É–º–º–∞ –≤ —Ä—É–±–ª—è—Ö
    total_usd REAL NOT NULL,  -- –°—É–º–º–∞ –≤ –¥–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä–∞—Ö
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,  -- –î–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1  -- –ê–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –ª–∏ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑
);
```

### –®–ê–ì 3: –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–ï BACKEND (–°–ï–†–í–ï–†–ù–ê–Ø –ß–ê–°–¢–¨)

Backend ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ "–º–æ—Å—Ç" –º–µ–∂–¥—É –±–∞–∑–æ–π –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–æ–º.

**–ß—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å:**
- –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å API (–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π)
- –ù–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã —Å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏:
  - –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏–∑ –±–∞–∑—ã
  - –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
  - –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—â–∏—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
  - –£–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤:**
```python
# backend/api/orders.py
from flask import Blueprint, jsonify
from backend.database import get_db

orders_bp = Blueprint('orders', __name__)

@orders_bp.route('/api/orders', methods=['GET'])
def get_orders():
    """–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤"""
    db = get_db()
    orders = db.execute('SELECT * FROM Orders').fetchall()
    
    # –ü—Ä–µ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—É–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–π–º–µ—Ç frontend
    orders_list = [
        {
            'id': order['id'],
            'status': order['status'],
            'description': order['description'],
            'total_cny': order['total_cny'],
            'total_rub': order['total_rub'],
            'total_usd': order['total_usd'],
            'created_at': order['created_at']
        }
        for order in orders
    ]
    
    return jsonify(orders_list)
```

### –®–ê–ì 4: –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–ï FRONTEND (–ò–ù–¢–ï–†–§–ï–ô–°)

Frontend ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å.

**–ß—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å:**
- –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã –∏ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—ã
- –ù–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥ –¥–ª—è –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
- –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ –∏ —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è
- –ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ —Å backend

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤:**
```javascript
// frontend/src/components/OrdersList.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const OrdersList = () => {
  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    // –ó–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —É backend
    fetch('/api/orders')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => {
        setOrders(data);
        setLoading(false);
      });
  }, []);

  if (loading) return <div>–ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤...</div>;

  return (
    <div className="orders-list">
      <h2>–°–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤</h2>
      
      <table>
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>‚Ññ –ó–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞</th>
            <th>–°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å</th>
            <th>–û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ</th>
            <th>–°—É–º–º–∞ (CNY)</th>
            <th>–°—É–º–º–∞ (RUB)</th>
            <th>–î–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {orders.map(order => (
            <tr key={order.id}>
              <td>{order.id}</td>
              <td>{order.status}</td>
              <td>{order.description}</td>
              <td>{order.total_cny.toFixed(2)}</td>
              <td>{order.total_rub.toFixed(2)}</td>
              <td>{new Date(order.created_at).toLocaleDateString()}</td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
};

export default OrdersList;
```

### –®–ê–ì 5: –°–í–Ø–ó–´–í–ê–ù–ò–ï BACKEND –ò FRONTEND

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–∏—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–µ.

**–ö–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç:**
1. –ü–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—É "–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑—ã" –≤ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–µ
2. Frontend –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∫ backend: `GET /api/orders`
3. Backend –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∏ –æ–±—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫ –±–∞–∑–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
4. –ë–∞–∑–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ö
5. Backend —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –∏—Ö –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ frontend
6. Frontend –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏ –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–∞–µ—Ç –∏—Ö –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ

### –®–ê–ì 6: –¢–ï–°–¢–ò–†–û–í–ê–ù–ò–ï –ò –î–û–†–ê–ë–û–¢–ö–ê

–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–æ–π —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ:
- –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤—Å–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ
- –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏
- –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—é—â–∏–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏
- –£–ª—É—á—à–∏—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å

## üîó –ö–ê–ö –í–°–Å –≠–¢–û –í–ó–ê–ò–ú–û–î–ï–ô–°–¢–í–£–ï–¢ –í "CARGO MANAGER –õ–ò–°–Å–ù–û–ö"

–î–∞–≤–∞–π —Ä–∞—Å—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä ‚Äî –∫–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫–∞ "–°–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è":

1. **–ë–∞–∑–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö:**
   - –ï—Å—Ç—å —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Communications` –¥–ª—è —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π
   - –ï—Å—Ç—å —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Orders` –¥–ª—è —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤
   - –ï—Å—Ç—å —Å–≤—è–∑—å –º–µ–∂–¥—É –Ω–∏–º–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ `order_id`

2. **Backend:**
   - –ï—Å—Ç—å —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è `get_messages_for_client(client_id)`, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è:

12. `Integrations` - –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Å –º–µ—Å—Å–µ–Ω–¥–∂–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏

## üóÉÔ∏è –î–ï–¢–ê–õ–¨–ù–û–ï –û–ü–ò–°–ê–ù–ò–ï –ö–ê–ñ–î–û–ô –¢–ê–ë–õ–ò–¶–´

### 1. –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Currencies` (–í–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã)

**–ù–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ**: –•—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞–µ–º—ã—Ö –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç–∞—Ö.

| –ü–æ–ª–µ | –¢–∏–ø | –û–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è | –û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ | –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è |
|------|-----|-------------|----------|----------------|
| id | INTEGER | PRIMARY KEY | –£–Ω–∏–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä | 1 |
| code | TEXT | NOT NULL, UNIQUE | –ö–æ–¥ –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã (ISO 4217) | "CNY", "RUB", "USD" |
| name | TEXT | NOT NULL | –ü–æ–ª–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã | "–ö–∏—Ç–∞–π—Å–∫–∏–π —é–∞–Ω—å", "–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä—É–±–ª—å", "–î–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä –°–®–ê" |
| symbol | TEXT | NOT NULL | –°–∏–º–≤–æ–ª –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã | "¬•", "‚ÇΩ", "$" |
| is_purchase_base | BOOLEAN | NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 | –Ø–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ª–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç–æ–π –∑–∞–∫—É–ø–æ–∫ | 1 –¥–ª—è CNY, 0 –¥–ª—è –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö |
| is_reporting_base | BOOLEAN | NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 | –Ø–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ª–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ–π –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç–æ–π | 1 –¥–ª—è RUB, 0 –¥–ª—è –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö |
| created_at | TIMESTAMP | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP | –î–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ | "2024-01-01 10:00:00" |

**–ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã**:
- PRIMARY KEY (id)
- UNIQUE (code)

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö**:
```sql

VALUES 
('CNY', '–ö–∏—Ç–∞–π—Å–∫–∏–π —é–∞–Ω—å', '¬•', 1, 0),
('RUB', '–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä—É–±–ª—å', '‚ÇΩ', 0, 1),
('USD', '–î–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä –°–®–ê', '$', 0, 0);
```

### 2. –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `CurrencyRates` (–ö—É—Ä—Å—ã –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç)

**–ù–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ**: –•—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö –∫—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç –¥–ª—è —Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å—á–µ—Ç–∞.

| –ü–æ–ª–µ | –¢–∏–ø | –û–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è | –û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ | –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è |
|------|-----|-------------|----------|----------------|
| id | INTEGER | PRIMARY KEY | –£–Ω–∏–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä | 1 |
| base_currency_id | INTEGER | NOT NULL | –°—Å—ã–ª–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—É—é –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—É | 1 (CNY) |
| target_currency_id | INTEGER | NOT NULL | –°—Å—ã–ª–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ü–µ–ª–µ–≤—É—é –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—É | 2 (RUB) |
| rate | REAL | NOT NULL | –ö—É—Ä—Å –æ–±–º–µ–Ω–∞ | 12.6 |
| date | DATE | NOT NULL | –î–∞—Ç–∞ –∫—É—Ä—Å–∞ | "2024-10-15" |
| source | TEXT | | –ò—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫ –∫—É—Ä—Å–∞ | "–¶–ë –†–§", "–ë–∞–Ω–∫ –†–æ—Å—Å–∏–∏" |
| created_at | TIMESTAMP | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP | –î–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ | "2024-10-15 10:00:00" |

**–ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã**:
- PRIMARY KEY (id)
- INDEX (base_currency_id)
- INDEX (target_currency_id)
- UNIQUE (base_currency_id, target_currency_id, date)

**–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö**:
```sql

-- –ö—É—Ä—Å CNY –∫ USD

VALUES (1, 3, 0.14, '2024-10-15');
```

### 7. –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `OrderProducts` (–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –≤ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ)

**–ù–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ**: –•—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞—Ö –≤ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–æ–º –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–µ.

### 12. –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Integrations` (–ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏)

**–ù–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ**: –•—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ–± –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ö —Å –º–µ—Å—Å–µ–Ω–¥–∂–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏.

| –ü–æ–ª–µ | –¢–∏–ø | –û–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è | –û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ | –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è |

### –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∏:
1. `Orders.client_id` ‚Üí `Clients.id`
2. `Orders.supplier_id` ‚Üí `Suppliers.id`
3. `Orders.id` ‚Üí `OrderProducts.order_id`
4. `Orders.id` ‚Üí `Shipments.order_id`
5. `Orders.id` ‚Üí `Documents.order_id`
6. `Orders.id` ‚Üí `Communications.order_id`
7. `Shipments.id` ‚Üí `ShipmentStages.shipment_id`
8. `CurrencyRates.base_currency_id` ‚Üí `Currencies.id`
9. `CurrencyRates.target_currency_id` ‚Üí `Currencies.id`

## üß± –¢–†–ò–ì–ì–ï–†–´ –î–õ–Ø –ê–í–¢–û–ú–ê–¢–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–û–ô –°–ò–ù–•–†–û–ù–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–ò

### 1. –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ —Å–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π —Å –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏
```sql
CREATE TRIGGER link_message_to_client
AFTER INSERT ON Communications
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    DECLARE client_id INT;
    
    -- –ü—ã—Ç–∞–µ–º—Å—è –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ø–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º
    SELECT id INTO client_id
    FROM Clients
    WHERE (telegram = (SELECT telegram FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id) OR
           whatsapp = (SELECT whatsapp FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id) OR
           phone = (SELECT phone FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id))
    LIMIT 1;
    
    -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω –∏ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –µ—â–µ –Ω–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–æ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–º, –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ
    IF client_id IS NOT NULL AND NEW.order_id IS NULL THEN
        -- –ù–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏–π –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
        SELECT id INTO @order_id
        FROM Orders
        WHERE client_id = client_id AND is_active = 1
        ORDER BY created_at DESC
        LIMIT 1;
        
        -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω, —Å–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–º
        IF @order_id IS NOT NULL THEN
            UPDATE Communications
            SET order_id = @order_id
            WHERE id = NEW.id;
        END IF;
    END IF;
END;
```

### 2. –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ –ø—Ä–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞
```sql
CREATE TRIGGER update_order_status_on_shipment
AFTER INSERT ON Shipments
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE Orders
    SET status = 'in_progress'
    WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
END;
```

### 3. –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤
```sql
CREATE TRIGGER update_order_status_on_completion
AFTER UPDATE ON Shipments
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    DECLARE active_shipments INT;
    
    -- –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º, –µ—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã –¥–ª—è —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO active_shipments
    FROM Shipments
    WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id AND current_status NOT IN ('–î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω', '–û—Ç–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω');
    
    -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤ –Ω–µ—Ç, —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ "–î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω"
    IF active_shipments = 0 THEN
        UPDATE Orders
        SET status = 'delivered'
        WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
    END IF;
END;
```

## üîç –ò–ù–î–ï–ö–°–´ –î–õ–Ø –û–ü–¢–ò–ú–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–ò –ü–û–ò–°–ö–ê

```sql
-- –ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã –¥–ª—è –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_client ON Orders(client_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_status ON Orders(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_active ON Orders(is_active);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_created ON Orders(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_expected_delivery ON Orders(expected_delivery);

-- –ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã –¥–ª—è –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤
CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_order ON Shipments(order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_status ON Shipments(current_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_expected_delivery ON Shipments(expected_delivery);

-- –ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã –¥–ª—è –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–π
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_order ON Communications(order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_contact ON Communications(contact_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_read ON Communications(read_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_direction ON Communications(direction);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_context ON Communications(context);
```

## üì¶ –ü–û–õ–ù–´–ô SQL-–°–ö–†–ò–ü–¢ –î–õ–Ø –°–û–ó–î–ê–ù–ò–Ø –ë–ê–ó–´ –î–ê–ù–ù–´–•

```sql
-- 1. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Currencies
CREATE TABLE Currencies (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    code TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_purchase_base BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    is_reporting_base BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 2. –ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ–º –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã
INSERT INTO Currencies (code, name, symbol, is_purchase_base, is_reporting_base)
VALUES 
('CNY', '–ö–∏—Ç–∞–π—Å–∫–∏–π —é–∞–Ω—å', '¬•', 1, 0),
('RUB', '–†–æ—Å—Å–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä—É–±–ª—å', '‚ÇΩ', 0, 1),
('USD', '–î–æ–ª–ª–∞—Ä –°–®–ê', '$', 0, 0);

-- 3. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É CurrencyRates
CREATE TABLE CurrencyRates (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    base_currency_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    target_currency_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    rate REAL NOT NULL,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    source TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (base_currency_id) REFERENCES Currencies(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (target_currency_id) REFERENCES Currencies(id),
    UNIQUE (base_currency_id, target_currency_id, date)
);

-- 4. –ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ–º –∫—É—Ä—Å—ã –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç
INSERT INTO CurrencyRates (base_currency_id, target_currency_id, rate, date)
VALUES 
(1, 2, 12.6, '2024-10-15'),
(1, 3, 0.14, '2024-10-15');

-- 5. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Clients
CREATE TABLE Clients (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    company TEXT,
    phone TEXT,
    telegram TEXT UNIQUE,
    whatsapp TEXT UNIQUE,
    wechat TEXT UNIQUE,
    email TEXT,
    is_new BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 6. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Suppliers
CREATE TABLE Suppliers (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    contact_person TEXT,
    phone TEXT,
    wechat TEXT UNIQUE,
    address TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 7. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É ProductCards
CREATE TABLE ProductCards (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    category TEXT,
    photo_url TEXT,
    weight_kg REAL,
    volume_m3 REAL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 8. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Orders
CREATE TABLE Orders (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    order_number TEXT UNIQUE,
    client_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    supplier_id INTEGER,
    status TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    total_cny REAL NOT NULL,
    total_rub REAL NOT NULL,
    total_usd REAL NOT NULL,
    weight_kg REAL,
    volume_m3 REAL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    expected_delivery DATETIME,
    actual_delivery DATETIME,
    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    FOREIGN KEY (client_id) REFERENCES Clients(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (supplier_id) REFERENCES Suppliers(id)
);

-- 9. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É OrderProducts
CREATE TABLE OrderProducts (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    order_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    product_card_id INTEGER,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    quantity INTEGER NOT NULL,
    price_cny REAL NOT NULL,
    photo_url TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (order_id) REFERENCES Orders(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (product_card_id) REFERENCES ProductCards(id)
);

-- 10. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Shipments
CREATE TABLE Shipments (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    order_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    shipment_number TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    carrier TEXT,
    current_status TEXT NOT NULL,
    location TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL,
    expected_delivery DATETIME,
    notes TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (order_id) REFERENCES Orders(id)
);

-- 11. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É ShipmentStages
CREATE TABLE ShipmentStages (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    shipment_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    stage TEXT NOT NULL,
    location TEXT NOT NULL,
    timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL,
    notes TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (shipment_id) REFERENCES Shipments(id)
);

-- 12. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Documents
CREATE TABLE Documents (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    order_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    type TEXT NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    content TEXT,
    file_url TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (order_id) REFERENCES Orders(id)
);

-- 13. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Communications
CREATE TABLE Communications (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    order_id TEXT,
    direction TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(direction IN ('incoming', 'outgoing')),
    channel TEXT NOT NULL,
    contact_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    message_text TEXT,
    attachments TEXT,
    read_status BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL,
    is_system BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    context TEXT,
    is_forwarded BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    original_message_id INTEGER,
    FOREIGN KEY (order_id) REFERENCES Orders(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (original_message_id) REFERENCES Communications(id)
);

-- 14. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É Integrations
CREATE TABLE Integrations (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    status TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(status IN ('active', 'pending', 'error', 'inactive')),
    config TEXT,
    last_connected TIMESTAMP,
    error_message TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 15. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É MessageTemplates
CREATE TABLE MessageTemplates (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    content_ru TEXT NOT NULL,
    content_zh TEXT,
    category TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(category IN ('–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å', '–ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ', '–∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è', '–ø–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π')),
    usage_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_used TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- 16. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã –¥–ª—è –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_client ON Orders(client_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_status ON Orders(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_active ON Orders(is_active);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_created ON Orders(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_orders_expected_delivery ON Orders(expected_delivery);

CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_order ON Shipments(order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_status ON Shipments(current_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_shipments_expected_delivery ON Shipments(expected_delivery);

CREATE INDEX idx_communications_order ON Communications(order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_contact ON Communications(contact_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_read ON Communications(read_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_direction ON Communications(direction);
CREATE INDEX idx_communications_context ON Communications(context);

-- 17. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ç—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä—ã –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–π —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏
CREATE TRIGGER link_message_to_client
AFTER INSERT ON Communications
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    DECLARE client_id INT;
    
    -- –ü—ã—Ç–∞–µ–º—Å—è –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ø–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º
    SELECT id INTO client_id
    FROM Clients
    WHERE (telegram = (SELECT telegram FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id) OR
           whatsapp = (SELECT whatsapp FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id) OR
           phone = (SELECT phone FROM Clients WHERE id = NEW.contact_id))
    LIMIT 1;
    
    -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω –∏ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –µ—â–µ –Ω–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–æ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–º, –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ
    IF client_id IS NOT NULL AND NEW.order_id IS NULL THEN
        -- –ù–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏–π –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
        SELECT id INTO @order_id
        FROM Orders
        WHERE client_id = client_id AND is_active = 1
        ORDER BY created_at DESC
        LIMIT 1;
        
        -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω, —Å–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ–º —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–º
        IF @order_id IS NOT NULL THEN
            UPDATE Communications
            SET order_id = @order_id
            WHERE id = NEW.id;
        END IF;
    END IF;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER update_order_status_on_shipment
AFTER INSERT ON Shipments
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE Orders
    SET status = 'in_progress'
    WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER update_order_status_on_completion
AFTER UPDATE ON Shipments
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    DECLARE active_shipments INT;
    
    -- –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º, –µ—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã –¥–ª—è —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO active_shipments
    FROM Shipments
    WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id AND current_status NOT IN ('–î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω', '–û—Ç–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω');
    
    -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤ –Ω–µ—Ç, —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ "–î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω"
    IF active_shipments = 0 THEN
        UPDATE Orders
        SET status = 'delivered'
        WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
    END IF;
END;
```

## ‚úÖ –ü–†–û–í–ï–†–ö–ê –°–¢–†–£–ö–¢–£–†–´ –ë–ê–ó–´ –î–ê–ù–ù–´–•

### 3. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Å–≤—è–∑–µ–π
1. –û—Ç–∫—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É `Orders`

### 4. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Ç—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä–æ–≤

2. –£–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç–µ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è `order_id` –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏–ª—Å—è
3. –î–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –Ω–æ–≤—ã–π –≥—Ä—É–∑ –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—É `Shipments`
4. –£–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç–µ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–∞ –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ `Orders` –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª—Å—è –Ω–∞ "in_progress"

## üí° –°–û–í–ï–¢–´ –ü–û –†–ê–ë–û–¢–ï –° –ë–ê–ó–û–ô –î–ê–ù–ù–´–•

1. **–†–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∫–æ–ø–∏–∏**: –†–µ–≥—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∫–æ–ø–∏–∏ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö
2. **–¢–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ**: –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏
3. **–ú–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏**: –ü—Ä–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç—ã –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏
4. **–ò–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã**: –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–π—Ç–µ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã –¥–ª—è —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º—ã—Ö –ø–æ–ª–µ–π
5. **–¢—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏**: –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–∏ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏—Ö –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π

## ü¶ä –ó–ê–ö–õ–Æ–ß–ï–ù–ò–ï

–≠—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö:
- **–ü–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å-–ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–∞–º** —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–∫–∞
- **–ò–∑–±–µ–≥–∞–µ—Ç –¥—É–±–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö** —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω–æ—Ä–º–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é
- **–û–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫** —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã
- **–ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ** —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —Ç—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä—ã
- **–ú–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è** –¥–ª—è –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–π

–° —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –±–∞–∑–æ–π –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –õ–∏—Å—ë–Ω–æ–∫ —Å–º–æ–∂–µ—Ç:

### 3. –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `OrderProducts` (–¢–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –≤ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–µ) - –ö–õ–Æ–ß–ï–í–ê–Ø –¢–ê–ë–õ–ò–¶–ê

**–ß—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç:**

- –û–±–µ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –æ–¥–Ω—É –∏ —Ç—É –∂–µ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É, –Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–µ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
- –≠—Ç–∞ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å –õ–Æ–ë–û–ï –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–µ

### 4. –ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç –æ–±—â–∏—Ö –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–≤

–ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è—é—Ç—Å—è —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –≤ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É, –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç:

```python
def update_order_totals(order_id):
    # –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –≤—Å–µ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ã –≤ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–µ
    order_products = db.execute("""
        SELECT * FROM OrderProducts 
        WHERE order_id = ?
    """, (order_id,)).fetchall()
    
    # –†–∞—Å—Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –æ–±—â–∏–µ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã
    total_cny = 0
    total_weight = 0
    total_volume = 0
    
    for product in order_products:
        total_cny += product['quantity'] * product['price_cny']
        total_weight += product['quantity'] * product['weight_kg']
        total_volume += product['quantity'] * product['volume_m3']
    
    # –ü–µ—Ä–µ—Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –≤ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ –≤–∞–ª—é—Ç—ã
    total_rub = convert_currency(total_cny, 'CNY', 'RUB')
    total_usd = convert_currency(total_cny, 'CNY', 'USD')
    
    # –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É
    db.execute("""
        UPDATE Orders 
        SET total_cny = ?, total_rub = ?, total_usd = ?, 
            weight_kg = ?, volume_m3 = ?
        WHERE id = ?
    """, (total_cny, total_rub, total_usd, total_weight, total_volume, order_id))
    
    # –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã
    update_documents_for_order(order_id)
```

- –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ª–µ–≥–∫–æ —Ä–µ–¥–∞–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ –±–µ–∑ –≤–ª–∏—è–Ω–∏—è –Ω–∞ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ

### 3. –ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π —Ä–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç
- –ü—Ä–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏/—É–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ –º–≥–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è—é—Ç—Å—è:
  - –û–±—â–∏–π –≤–µ—Å –∏ –æ–±—ä–µ–º

  - –ü–ª–æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≥—Ä—É–∑–∞

  - –î–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–ª—è –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤

### 4. –£–¥–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–æ –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è

## üß± –¢–ï–•–ù–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–ê–Ø –†–ï–ê–õ–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø

### SQL-–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ –≤ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–µ
```sql
SELECT 
    op.id,
    op.quantity,
    op.price_cny,
    pc.name,
    pc.description,
    pc.category,
    pc.weight_kg,
    pc.volume_m3,
    pc.photo_url
FROM OrderProducts op
JOIN ProductCards pc ON op.product_card_id = pc.id
WHERE op.order_id = '2024-110'
ORDER BY op.created_at DESC;
```

### –¢—Ä–∏–≥–≥–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
```sql
CREATE TRIGGER update_order_after_product_change
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON OrderProducts
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    -- –î–ª—è INSERT –∏ UPDATE
    IF NEW.order_id IS NOT NULL THEN
        UPDATE Orders
        SET 
            total_cny = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * price_cny) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id
            ),
            weight_kg = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * weight_kg) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                JOIN ProductCards ON OrderProducts.product_card_id = ProductCards.id
                WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id
            ),
            volume_m3 = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * volume_m3) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                JOIN ProductCards ON OrderProducts.product_card_id = ProductCards.id
                WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id
            )
        WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
    END IF;
    
    -- –î–ª—è DELETE
    IF OLD.order_id IS NOT NULL AND NEW.order_id IS NULL THEN
        UPDATE Orders
        SET 
            total_cny = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * price_cny) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                WHERE order_id = OLD.order_id
            ),
            weight_kg = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * weight_kg) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                JOIN ProductCards ON OrderProducts.product_card_id = ProductCards.id
                WHERE order_id = OLD.order_id
            ),
            volume_m3 = (
                SELECT SUM(quantity * volume_m3) 
                FROM OrderProducts 
                JOIN ProductCards ON OrderProducts.product_card_id = ProductCards.id
                WHERE order_id = OLD.order_id
            )
        WHERE id = OLD.order_id;
    END IF;
END;
```

## ü¶ä –ó–ê–ö–õ–Æ–ß–ï–ù–ò–ï

### USER
